  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV TZ=UTC

      python3.8 \

  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade pip
  RUN pip3 install torch==1.4.0+cpu torchvision==0.5.0+cpu -f https://download.pytorch.org/whl/torch_stable.html || \
      pip3 install torch==1.4.0 torchvision==0.5.0

      numpy==1.17.2 \
      matplotlib==3.1.1 \
      tqdm==4.36.1 \

      scipy==1.3.1 \

      Pillow==6.2.0 \

      pyparsing==2.4.2 \

      six==1.12.0
  RUN mkdir -p data dumps saves plots/lt/combined_plots plots/reinit runs
  RUN echo "__pycache__/\n*.pyc\ndata/\ndumps/\nsaves/\nplots/\nruns/\n.DS_Store\n*.pth\n*.log" > .gitignore
  RUN echo "import torch\nimport torchvision\nimport numpy\nimport matplotlib\nimport tqdm\nimport pandas\nimport seaborn\nimport scipy\nimport tensorboardX\nfrom PIL import Image\nprint('All imports successful')\nprint(f'PyTorch version: {torch.__version__}')\nprint(f'CUDA available: {torch.cuda.is_available()}')\nprint('Running in CPU-only mode')" > test_main.py
  RUN echo "# Configuration settings\nDEVICE = 'cpu'\nBATCH_SIZE = 64\nLEARNING_RATE = 0.001\nEPOCHS = 10" > config.py
  ENV PYTHONUNBUFFERED=1
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

  #5 22.57  This PPA contains more recent Python versions packaged for Ubuntu.
  #5 22.57 
  #5 22.57 Disclaimer: there's no guarantee of timely updates in case of security problems or other issues. If you want to use them in a security-or-otherwise-critical environment (say, on a production server), you do so at your own risk.
  #5 22.57 
  #5 22.57 Update Note
  #5 22.57 ===========
  #5 22.57 Please use this repository instead of ppa:fkrull/deadsnakes.
  #5 22.57 
  #5 22.57 Reporting Issues
  #5 22.57 ================
  #5 22.57 
  #5 22.57 Issues can be reported in the master issue tracker at:
  #5 22.57 https://github.com/deadsnakes/issues/issues
  #5 22.57 
  #5 22.57 Supported Ubuntu and Python Versions
  #5 22.57 ====================================
  #5 22.57 
  #5 22.57 - Ubuntu 20.04 (focal) Python3.5 - Python3.7, Python3.9 - Python3.13
  #5 22.57 - Ubuntu 22.04 (jammy) Python3.7 - Python3.9, Python3.11 - Python3.13
  #5 22.57 - Ubuntu 24.04 (noble) Python3.7 - Python3.11, Python3.13
  #5 22.57 - Note: Python2.7 (focal, jammy), Python 3.8 (focal), Python 3.10 (jammy), Python3.12 (noble) are not provided by deadsnakes as upstream ubuntu provides those packages.
  #5 22.57 
  #5 22.57 Why some packages aren't built:
  #5 22.57 - Note: for focal, older python versions require libssl<1.1 so they are not currently built
  #5 22.57 - Note: for jammy and noble, older python versions requre libssl<3 so they are not currently built
  #5 22.57 - If you need these, reach out to asottile to set up a private ppa
  #5 22.57 
  #5 22.57 The packages may also work on other versions of Ubuntu or Debian, but that is not tested or supported.
  #5 22.57 
  #5 22.57 Packages
  #5 22.57 ========
  #5 22.57 
  #5 22.57 The packages provided here are loosely based on the debian upstream packages with some modifications to make them more usable as non-default pythons and on ubuntu.  As such, the packages follow debian's patterns and often do not include a full python distribution with just `apt install python#.#`.  Here is a list of packages that may be useful along with the default install:
  #5 22.57 
  #5 22.57 - `python#.#-dev`: includes development headers for building C extensions
  #5 22.57 - `python#.#-venv`: provides the standard library `venv` module
  #5 22.57 - `python#.#-distutils`: provides the standard library `distutils` module
  #5 22.57 - `python#.#-lib2to3`: provides the `2to3-#.#` utility as well as the standard library `lib2to3` module
  #5 22.57 - `python#.#-gdbm`: provides the standard library `dbm.gnu` module
  #5 22.57 - `python#.#-tk`: provides the standard library `tkinter` module
  #5 22.57 
  #5 22.57 Third-Party Python Modules
  #5 22.57 ==========================
  #5 22.57 
  #5 22.57 Python modules in the official Ubuntu repositories are packaged to work with the Python interpreters from the official repositories. Accordingly, they generally won't work with the Python interpreters from this PPA. As an exception, pure-Python modules for Python 3 will work, but any compiled extension modules won't.
  #5 22.57 
  #5 22.57 To install 3rd-party Python modules, you should use the common Python packaging tools.  For an introduction into the Python packaging ecosystem and its tools, refer to the Python Packaging User Guide:
  #5 22.57 https://packaging.python.org/installing/
  #5 22.57 
  #5 22.57 Sources
  #5 22.57 =======
  #5 22.57 The package sources are available at:
  #5 22.57 https://github.com/deadsnakes/
  #5 22.57

      python3.7 get-pip.py && \
      rm get-pip.py
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Lottory
  RUN git clone https://github.com/rahulvigneswaran/Lottery-Ticket-Hypothesis-in-Pytorch.git . || true
  RUN python3.7 -m pip install --upgrade pip
  RUN python3.7 -m pip install torch==1.2.0+cpu torchvision==0.4.0+cpu -f https://download.pytorch.org/whl/torch_stable.html || \
      python3.7 -m pip install torch==1.2.0 torchvision==0.4.0
  RUN python3.7 -m pip install numpy==1.17.2

  RUN python3.7 -m pip install pytz==2019.2

  RUN mkdir -p data dumps saves plots/lt/combined_plots plots/reinit runs

  RUN echo "import torch\nimport torchvision\nimport numpy\nimport matplotlib\nimport tqdm\nimport pandas\nimport seaborn\nimport scipy\nimport tensorboardX\nfrom PIL import Image\nprint('All imports successful')\nprint(f'PyTorch version: {torch.__version__}')\nprint(f'CUDA available: {torch.cuda.is_available()}')\nprint('Running in CPU-only mode')" > test_main.py
  RUN echo "# Configuration settings\nDEVICE = 'cpu'\nBATCH_SIZE = 64\nLEARNING_RATE = 0.001\nEPOCHS = 10" > config.py
  ENV PYTHONUNBUFFERED=1
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:20.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV TZ=UTC
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      software-properties-common \
      && add-apt-repository ppa:deadsnakes/ppa \
      && apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      python3.7 \
      python3.7-dev \
      python3.7-distutils \
      git \
      wget \
      curl \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN curl https://bootstrap.pypa.io/pip/3.7/get-pip.py -o get-pip.py && \
      python3.7 get-pip.py && \
      rm get-pip.py
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Lottory
  RUN git clone https://github.com/rahulvigneswaran/Lottery-Ticket-Hypothesis-in-Pytorch.git . || true
  RUN python3.7 -m pip install --upgrade pip
  RUN python3.7 -m pip install torch==1.2.0+cpu torchvision==0.4.0+cpu -f https://download.pytorch.org/whl/torch_stable.html || \
      python3.7 -m pip install torch==1.2.0 torchvision==0.4.0
  RUN python3.7 -m pip install numpy==1.17.2
  RUN python3.7 -m pip install matplotlib==3.1.1
  RUN python3.7 -m pip install tqdm==4.36.1
  RUN python3.7 -m pip install pandas==0.25.1
  RUN python3.7 -m pip install seaborn==0.9.0
  RUN python3.7 -m pip install scipy==1.3.1
  RUN python3.7 -m pip install tensorboardX==1.8
  RUN python3.7 -m pip install Pillow==6.2.0
  RUN python3.7 -m pip install cycler==0.10.0
  RUN python3.7 -m pip install kiwisolver==1.1.0
  RUN python3.7 -m pip install protobuf==3.9.2
  RUN python3.7 -m pip install pyparsing==2.4.2
  RUN python3.7 -m pip install python-dateutil==2.8.0
  RUN python3.7 -m pip install pytz==2019.2
  RUN python3.7 -m pip install six==1.12.0
